(NASDAQ: KTEC) announced today sales and operating results for its fiscal </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter, ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Third</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Quarter Overview</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Net sales for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;totaled </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$30.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$31.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;recorded in the corresponding quarter last year.  The Company reported net earnings for the quarter of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$295,000</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$0.05</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;per diluted share, compared to a net loss of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$2.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$0.32</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;per diluted share, in the same period a year ago.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The gross profit for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">third quarter of fiscal</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$9.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$8.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the corresponding period last year.  As a percentage of net sales, gross profit was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">30.0%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">26.0%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">third quarter of fiscal</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, respectively. respectively.  Operating expenses for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">nine-month period ended</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$25.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">35.8%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net sales, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$32.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">37.8%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of net sales, for the corresponding period of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Jack Ehren, President and CEO, commented, &#8220;Our gross margin percentage in the third quarter of fiscal 2015 increased, compared to the third quarter of fiscal 2014, primarily due to favorable facility utilization in fiscal 2015, and the absence of the workforce reduction-related charges that were incurred in the third quarter of fiscal 2014.  Our year-to-date gross margin percentage remained lower than historical levels due to lower net sales and production levels, and a less favorable product mix.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Ehren further commented, &#8220;We continue to manage our overall cost structure and, as a result, our fiscal year 2015 operating expenses, both for the third quarter and year-to-date, have continued to decline significantly in all functional areas, compared to the same periods in the prior fiscal year.  The cost savings realized from the workforce reductions implemented in the third quarter of fiscal 2014 and the </font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sC75DBAD8DBE93AC430EBB60201D99702"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter of fiscal 2015, as well as anticipated lower R&amp;D project expenses, are the main contributors to the lower expense levels in fiscal 2015.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Orders and Backlog</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Key's backlog at the end of the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">third quarter of fiscal</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$29.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$26.6 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;one year ago.  New orders received during the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;quarter were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$28.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$26.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the corresponding period last year.  New orders for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">nine months ended</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$84.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$86.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the corresponding period in fiscal </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Ehren stated, &#8220;The European market is a high-priority strategic focus for the Company.  In the third quarter, our European orders in euros achieved a quarterly record for this region, with several strategic wins across all core market segments.  North American orders remained sluggish in the third quarter, primarily due to a slow-down in capital investment and project delays in our core segments.  Globally, there are multiple significant projects for which we were expecting to receive orders in the fourth quarter, primarily in the potato market, which have now been delayed into fiscal 2016 and beyond.  As a result, we no longer expect to achieve year-over-year double-digit bookings growth in fiscal 2015.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Conclusion</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Ehren concluded, &#8220;We remain confident in our long-term strategic direction, and in our ability to effectively leverage the investments we have made over the past few years to drive anticipated profitable growth and increased shareholder value in the future.  We are currently engaged in extensive field-testing of our new developments in our core segments in Europe and North America, and we continue to expect to bring these developments to market in late fiscal 2015.  We are encouraged by the response of our strategic partners to the value of our new solutions, and we are confident in our ability to effectively leverage these developments in penetrating new and existing insertion points in our core and high-potential adjacent markets.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font Technology</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Key Technology (NASDAQ: KTEC</font><font Key offers customer demonstration and testing services at five locations including Walla Walla, Beusichem, and Hasselt</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#1f497d;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">as well as Sacramento, California, USA and Melbourne, Australia; and maintains a sales and service office in Santiago de Queretaro, Mexico.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Certain statements in this press release may be forward-looking statements for purposes of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
